Infrastructure Audit\\n\\n### Overview\\nArangoDB implements a comprehensive authentication and authorization system for protecting database operations. The infrastructure spans multiple layers: HTTP request authentication, user credential validation, permission caching, and execution context tracking.\\n\\n### 1. User Authentication Implementation\\n\\n**Primary Authentication Handler: `UserManager` (arangod/Auth/UserManager.h)**\\n- Abstract base class defining the interface for user and permission management\\n- Sole point of access for users and permissions stored in `_system/_users` collection\\n- Key methods:\\n  - `checkCredentials(username, token)` - Verifies user credentials\\n  - `createRootUser()` - Creates default root user\\n  - `storeUser()` - Stores user credentials\\n  - `removeUser()` - Removes user from system\\n  - `databaseAuthLevel()` - Checks user's database permissions\\n  - `collectionAuthLevel()` - Checks user's collection permissions\\n\\n**Implementation: `UserManagerImpl` (arangod/Auth/UserManagerImpl.h)**\\n- Concrete implementation of UserManager\\n- Manages user caching and background update thread\\n- Only exists on coordinators and single servers (not on DBServers)\\n- Loads user cache from `_system/_users` collection and maintains it locally\\n- Methods:\\n  - `loadUserCacheAndStartUpdateThread()` - Loads initial user cache and starts update thread\\n  - `triggerGlobalReload()` - Triggers reload on all coordinators\\n  - `enumerateUsers()`, `accessUser()`, `updateUser()` - User management operations\\n\\n### 2. JWT Token Validation for REST API\\n\\n**Token Validation: `TokenCache` (arangod/Auth/TokenCache.h and .cpp)**\\n- Caches both basic HTTP authentication and JWT authentication tokens\\n- Methods for JWT validation:\\n  - `checkAuthentication(authType, mode, secret)` - Main entry point for authentication\\n  - `checkAuthenticationJWT(secret)` - Validates JWT tokens\\n  - `validateJwtHeader()` - Parses and validates JWT header\\n  - `validateJwtBody()` - Parses and validates JWT payload\\n  - `validateJwtHMAC256Signature()` - Validates HMAC-SHA256 signatures\\n  - `validateJwtES256Signature()` - Validates ES256 (ECDSA) signatures\\n- Supports both HMAC256 and ES256 (elliptic curve) JWT signing algorithms\\n- Maintains LRU cache for JWT tokens to avoid repeated validation\\n- Entry structure includes: username, expiry time, authenticated flag, roles, allowed paths, and JWT token string\\n\\n**Authentication Feature: `AuthenticationFeature` (arangod/GeneralServer/AuthenticationFeature.h and .cpp)**\\n- Application feature managing authentication configuration and initialization\\n- Manages TokenCache instance and UserManager singleton\\n- Loads JWT secrets from files or folders\\n- Methods:\\n  - `isActive()` - Checks if authentication is enabled\\n  - `tokenCache()` - Returns reference to token cache\\n  - `userManager()` - Returns pointer to user manager\\n  - `jwtSecrets()` - Returns active and passive JWT secrets\\n  - `loadJwtSecretsFromFile()` - Loads secrets from specified file\\n  - `loadJwtSecretFolder()` - Loads secrets from folder (alphabetically sorted)\\n\\n### 3. Authorization Context for Permission Checks\\n\\n**Execution Context: `ExecContext` (arangod/Utils/ExecContext.h and .cpp)**\\n- Central mechanism for tracking execution context and permissions\\n- Thread-local static variable `ExecContext::CURRENT` holds current execution context\\n- Inherits from RequestContext for convenience\\n- Key components:\\n  - User identity (username)\\n  - Database context\\n  - Authentication levels: system database level and current database level\\n  - JWT token and roles (if authenticated via JWT)\\n  - Admin user flag\\n\\n**Authorization Methods:**\\n- `canUseDatabase(auth::Level requested)` - Checks if user can access database with given permission level\\n- `canUseCollection(dbname, collection, auth::Level requested)` - Checks collection access\\n- `collectionAuthLevel(dbname, collection)` - Returns user's auth level for specific collection\\n- `isAdminUser()` - Checks if user has admin privileges\\n- `isSuperuser()` - Checks if context represents internal superuser\\n- `isReadOnly()` - Checks if context is read-only internal user\\n\\n**Auth Level Hierarchy (arangod/Auth/Common.h):**\\n- `UNDEFINED = 0` - No access level defined\\n- `NONE = 1` - No access\\n- `RO = 2` - Read-only access\\n- `RW = 3` - Read-write access\\n\\n**User Permissions Model (arangod/Auth/User.h):**\\n- User class represents a user entry with access levels for databases and collections\\n- Methods:\\n  - `checkPassword()` - Validates user password\\n  - `updatePassword()` - Updates user password\\n  - `grantDatabase()`, `removeDatabase()` - Manages database permissions\\n  - `grantCollection()`, `removeCollection()` - Manages collection permissions\\n  - `databaseAuthLevel()`, `collectionAuthLevel()` - Resolves effective permissions\\n  - `checkAccessToken()` - Validates access tokens\\n  - Support for special \\\"*\\\" wildcard for default database/collection permissions\\n\\n### 4. REST API User Management Endpoint\\n\\n**User Management Handler: `RestUsersHandler` (arangod/RestHandler/RestUsersHandler.h and .cpp)**\\n- Implements `/_api/user` REST endpoint for user management\\n- Supports all HTTP methods: GET, POST, PUT, PATCH, DELETE\\n- Methods:\\n  - `getRequest()` - Retrieves user information\\n  - `postRequest()` - Creates new user\\n  - `putRequest()` - Replaces user\\n  - `patchRequest()` - Updates user properties\\n  - `deleteRequest()` - Removes user\\n  - `generateDatabaseResult()` - Generates response with database permissions\\n  - `generateUserResult()` - Formats user response\\n- Supports special paths like:\\n  - `/_api/user/<user>/database/<dbname>` - Get specific database permissions\\n  - `/_api/user/<user>/database?full=true/false` - Get all database permissions\\n  - `/_api/user/<user>/config` - Get user configuration (WebUI)\\n- Exceptions allow unauthorized users to call `/_api/user/<name>` to check passwords\\n\\n**Authentication Endpoint: `RestAuthHandler` (arangod/RestHandler/RestAuthHandler.h and .cpp)**\\n- Implements `/_open/auth` REST endpoint for JWT token generation\\n- Accepts POST requests with username and password\\n- Returns JWT token with configurable expiry time\\n- Methods:\\n  - `execute()` - Processes authentication request\\n  - `generateJwt()` - Generates JWT token for authenticated user\\n  - `badRequest()` - Returns 400 error response\\n- Supports token renewal endpoint\\n\\n### 5. Authentication Configuration and Defaults\\n\\n**Configuration Options (arangod/GeneralServer/AuthenticationOptions.h):**\\n\\nDefault values:\\n- `authenticationUnixSockets = true` - Enable auth for UNIX sockets\\n- `authenticationSystemOnly = true` - Only allow system database access during setup\\n- `active = true` - Authentication enabled by default\\n- `externalRBACservice = \\\"\\\"` - No external RBAC (Enterprise only)\\n- `authenticationTimeout = 0.0` - No timeout for cache (indefinite)\\n- `sessionTimeout = 3600.0` - 1 hour session timeout for web interface\\n- `minimalJwtExpiryTime = 10.0` - Minimum 10 seconds for JWT expiry\\n- `maximalJwtExpiryTime = 3600.0` - Maximum 1 hour for JWT expiry\\n- `jwtSecretIsES256 = false` - Default HMAC256, can use ES256\\n\\n**Startup Options (arangod/GeneralServer/AuthenticationFeature.cpp):**\\n- `--server.authentication` - Enable/disable authentication (default: true)\\n- `--server.authentication-timeout` - Cache timeout in seconds (default: 0)\\n- `--server.session-timeout` - Web interface JWT lifetime (default: 3600 seconds)\\n- `--server.authentication-unix-sockets` - Auth for UNIX sockets (default: true)\\n- `--server.authentication-system-only` - System-only auth mode\\n- `--server.jwt-secret` - JWT secret for signing tokens\\n- `--server.jwt-secret-keyfile` - Path to JWT secret keyfile\\n- `--server.jwt-secret-folder` - Folder containing JWT secrets\\n- `--auth.minimal-jwt-expiry-time` - Minimum JWT expiry (default: 1.0 seconds)\\n- `--auth.maximal-jwt-expiry-time` - Maximum JWT expiry (default: 3600.0 seconds)\\n\\n**JWT Secret Management:**\\n- Supports both inline secrets and file/folder-based secrets\\n- Folder-based secrets sorted alphabetically: first secret is active (for signing), others are passive (verification only)\\n- Supports HMAC256 (raw secret) and ES256 (PEM-formatted EC private key)\\n- Can be reloaded via `POST /_admin/server/jwt` without restart\\n\\n### 6. Request Authentication Flow\\n\\n**HTTP Request Handler: `CommTask` (arangod/GeneralServer/CommTask.h and .cpp)**\\n- Central HTTP request processor that applies authentication\\n- `prepareExecution()` method checks authentication and returns Flow decision\\n- Automatic exceptions for certain endpoints like `/_api/user/<name>` to allow password checking\\n- Calls `TokenCache::checkAuthentication()` to validate credentials\\n- Extracts username, roles, and JWT token from authentication result\\n- Sets ExecContext with user information and permissions\\n\\n**Authentication Handler Interface (arangod/Auth/Handler.h)**\\n- Abstract base class for pluggable authentication handlers\\n- Methods:\\n  - `authenticate(username, password)` - Authenticates and returns user roles\\n  - `readPermissions(username)` - Reads user permissions\\n  - Used by TokenCache for user validation\\n\\n### Summary of Key Components\\n\\n| Component | File | Role |\\n|-----------|------|------|\\n| UserManager | arangod/Auth/UserManager.h | Abstract user/permission access interface |\\n| UserManagerImpl | arangod/Auth/UserManagerImpl.h | Concrete implementation with caching |\\n| ExecContext | arangod/Utils/ExecContext.h | Execution context with permission tracking |\\n| AuthenticationFeature | arangod/GeneralServer/AuthenticationFeature.h | Configuration and initialization |\\n| RestAuthHandler | arangod/RestHandler/RestAuthHandler.h | JWT token generation endpoint |\\n| RestUsersHandler | arangod/RestHandler/RestUsersHandler.h | User management endpoint |\\n| TokenCache | arangod/Auth/TokenCache.h | Token validation and caching |\\n| AuthenticationOptions | arangod/GeneralServer/AuthenticationOptions.h | Configuration defaults |\\n| CommTask | arangod/GeneralServer/CommTask.h | HTTP request authentication processor |\\n| User | arangod/Auth/User.h | User entity with password and permission storage |\\n| Handler | arangod/Auth/Handler.h | Pluggable authentication interface |\\n| Common | arangod/Auth/Common.h | Auth level enums and utilities |\\n\\n### Design Patterns\\n\\n1. **Singleton Pattern**: AuthenticationFeature and ExecContext use singleton/thread-local patterns\\n2. **Strategy Pattern**: Handler interface allows different authentication backends\\n3. **Caching Strategy**: TokenCache uses LRU cache for JWT tokens and basic auth credentials\\n4. **Scope Guard Pattern**: ExecContextScope and ExecContextSuperuserScope manage context lifecycle\\n5. **Feature Pattern**: AuthenticationFeature integrates into application feature system\\n\\nThe architecture ensures secure authentication and fine-grained authorization at multiple layers, from HTTP request entry points through permission resolution for database Infrastructure Audit\\n\\n### Overview\\nArangoDB implements a comprehensive authentication and authorization system for protecting database operations. The infrastructure spans multiple layers: HTTP request authentication, user credential validation, permission caching, and execution context tracking.\\n\\n### 1. User Authentication Implementation\\n\\n**Primary Authentication Handler: `UserManager` (arangod/Auth/UserManager.h)**\\n- Abstract base class defining the interface for user and permission management\\n- Sole point of access for users and permissions stored in `_system/_users` collection\\n- Key methods:\\n  - `checkCredentials(username, token)` - Verifies user credentials\\n  - `createRootUser()` - Creates default root user\\n  - `storeUser()` - Stores user credentials\\n  - `removeUser()` - Removes user from system\\n  - `databaseAuthLevel()` - Checks user's database permissions\\n  - `collectionAuthLevel()` - Checks user's collection permissions\\n\\n**Implementation: `UserManagerImpl` (arangod/Auth/UserManagerImpl.h)**\\n- Concrete implementation of UserManager\\n- Manages user caching and background update thread\\n- Only exists on coordinators and single servers (not on DBServers)\\n- Loads user cache from `_system/_users` collection and maintains it locally\\n- Methods:\\n  - `loadUserCacheAndStartUpdateThread()` - Loads initial user cache and starts update thread\\n  - `triggerGlobalReload()` - Triggers reload on all coordinators\\n  - `enumerateUsers()`, `accessUser()`, `updateUser()` - User management operations\\n\\n### 2. JWT Token Validation for REST API\\n\\n**Token Validation: `TokenCache` (arangod/Auth/TokenCache.h and .cpp)**\\n- Caches both basic HTTP authentication and JWT authentication tokens\\n- Methods for JWT validation:\\n  - `checkAuthentication(authType, mode, secret)` - Main entry point for authentication\\n  - `checkAuthenticationJWT(secret)` - Validates JWT tokens\\n  - `validateJwtHeader()` - Parses and validates JWT header\\n  - `validateJwtBody()` - Parses and validates JWT payload\\n  - `validateJwtHMAC256Signature()` - Validates HMAC-SHA256 signatures\\n  - `validateJwtES256Signature()` - Validates ES256 (ECDSA) signatures\\n- Supports both HMAC256 and ES256 (elliptic curve) JWT signing algorithms\\n- Maintains LRU cache for JWT tokens to avoid repeated validation\\n- Entry structure includes: username, expiry time, authenticated flag, roles, allowed paths, and JWT token string\\n\\n**Authentication Feature: `AuthenticationFeature` (arangod/GeneralServer/AuthenticationFeature.h and .cpp)**\\n- Application feature managing authentication configuration and initialization\\n- Manages TokenCache instance and UserManager singleton\\n- Loads JWT secrets from files or folders\\n- Methods:\\n  - `isActive()` - Checks if authentication is enabled\\n  - `tokenCache()` - Returns reference to token cache\\n  - `userManager()` - Returns pointer to user manager\\n  - `jwtSecrets()` - Returns active and passive JWT secrets\\n  - `loadJwtSecretsFromFile()` - Loads secrets from specified file\\n  - `loadJwtSecretFolder()` - Loads secrets from folder (alphabetically sorted)\\n\\n### 3. Authorization Context for Permission Checks\\n\\n**Execution Context: `ExecContext` (arangod/Utils/ExecContext.h and .cpp)**\\n- Central mechanism for tracking execution context and permissions\\n- Thread-local static variable `ExecContext::CURRENT` holds current execution context\\n- Inherits from RequestContext for convenience\\n- Key components:\\n  - User identity (username)\\n  - Database context\\n  - Authentication levels: system database level and current database level\\n  - JWT token and roles (if authenticated via JWT)\\n  - Admin user flag\\n\\n**Authorization Methods:**\\n- `canUseDatabase(auth::Level requested)` - Checks if user can access database with given permission level\\n- `canUseCollection(dbname, collection, auth::Level requested)` - Checks collection access\\n- `collectionAuthLevel(dbname, collection)` - Returns user's auth level for specific collection\\n- `isAdminUser()` - Checks if user has admin privileges\\n- `isSuperuser()` - Checks if context represents internal superuser\\n- `isReadOnly()` - Checks if context is read-only internal user\\n\\n**Auth Level Hierarchy (arangod/Auth/Common.h):**\\n- `UNDEFINED = 0` - No access level defined\\n- `NONE = 1` - No access\\n- `RO = 2` - Read-only access\\n- `RW = 3` - Read-write access\\n\\n**User Permissions Model (arangod/Auth/User.h):**\\n- User class represents a user entry with access levels for databases and collections\\n- Methods:\\n  - `checkPassword()` - Validates user password\\n  - `updatePassword()` - Updates user password\\n  - `grantDatabase()`, `removeDatabase()` - Manages database permissions\\n  - `grantCollection()`, `removeCollection()` - Manages collection permissions\\n  - `databaseAuthLevel()`, `collectionAuthLevel()` - Resolves effective permissions\\n  - `checkAccessToken()` - Validates access tokens\\n  - Support for special \\\"*\\\" wildcard for default database/collection permissions\\n\\n### 4. REST API User Management Endpoint\\n\\n**User Management Handler: `RestUsersHandler` (arangod/RestHandler/RestUsersHandler.h and .cpp)**\\n- Implements `/_api/user` REST endpoint for user management\\n- Supports all HTTP methods: GET, POST, PUT, PATCH, DELETE\\n- Methods:\\n  - `getRequest()` - Retrieves user information\\n  - `postRequest()` - Creates new user\\n  - `putRequest()` - Replaces user\\n  - `patchRequest()` - Updates user properties\\n  - `deleteRequest()` - Removes user\\n  - `generateDatabaseResult()` - Generates response with database permissions\\n  - `generateUserResult()` - Formats user response\\n- Supports special paths like:\\n  - `/_api/user/<user>/database/<dbname>` - Get specific database permissions\\n  - `/_api/user/<user>/database?full=true/false` - Get all database permissions\\n  - `/_api/user/<user>/config` - Get user configuration (WebUI)\\n- Exceptions allow unauthorized users to call `/_api/user/<name>` to check passwords\\n\\n**Authentication Endpoint: `RestAuthHandler` (arangod/RestHandler/RestAuthHandler.h and .cpp)**\\n- Implements `/_open/auth` REST endpoint for JWT token generation\\n- Accepts POST requests with username and password\\n- Returns JWT token with configurable expiry time\\n- Methods:\\n  - `execute()` - Processes authentication request\\n  - `generateJwt()` - Generates JWT token for authenticated user\\n  - `badRequest()` - Returns 400 error response\\n- Supports token renewal endpoint\\n\\n### 5. Authentication Configuration and Defaults\\n\\n**Configuration Options (arangod/GeneralServer/AuthenticationOptions.h):**\\n\\nDefault values:\\n- `authenticationUnixSockets = true` - Enable auth for UNIX sockets\\n- `authenticationSystemOnly = true` - Only allow system database access during setup\\n- `active = true` - Authentication enabled by default\\n- `externalRBACservice = \\\"\\\"` - No external RBAC (Enterprise only)\\n- `authenticationTimeout = 0.0` - No timeout for cache (indefinite)\\n- `sessionTimeout = 3600.0` - 1 hour session timeout for web interface\\n- `minimalJwtExpiryTime = 10.0` - Minimum 10 seconds for JWT expiry\\n- `maximalJwtExpiryTime = 3600.0` - Maximum 1 hour for JWT expiry\\n- `jwtSecretIsES256 = false` - Default HMAC256, can use ES256\\n\\n**Startup Options (arangod/GeneralServer/AuthenticationFeature.cpp):**\\n- `--server.authentication` - Enable/disable authentication (default: true)\\n- `--server.authentication-timeout` - Cache timeout in seconds (default: 0)\\n- `--server.session-timeout` - Web interface JWT lifetime (default: 3600 seconds)\\n- `--server.authentication-unix-sockets` - Auth for UNIX sockets (default: true)\\n- `--server.authentication-system-only` - System-only auth mode\\n- `--server.jwt-secret` - JWT secret for signing tokens\\n- `--server.jwt-secret-keyfile` - Path to JWT secret keyfile\\n- `--server.jwt-secret-folder` - Folder containing JWT secrets\\n- `--auth.minimal-jwt-expiry-time` - Minimum JWT expiry (default: 1.0 seconds)\\n- `--auth.maximal-jwt-expiry-time` - Maximum JWT expiry (default: 3600.0 seconds)\\n\\n**JWT Secret Management:**\\n- Supports both inline secrets and file/folder-based secrets\\n- Folder-based secrets sorted alphabetically: first secret is active (for signing), others are passive (verification only)\\n- Supports HMAC256 (raw secret) and ES256 (PEM-formatted EC private key)\\n- Can be reloaded via `POST /_admin/server/jwt` without restart\\n\\n### 6. Request Authentication Flow\\n\\n**HTTP Request Handler: `CommTask` (arangod/GeneralServer/CommTask.h and .cpp)**\\n- Central HTTP request processor that applies authentication\\n- `prepareExecution()` method checks authentication and returns Flow decision\\n- Automatic exceptions for certain endpoints like `/_api/user/<name>` to allow password checking\\n- Calls `TokenCache::checkAuthentication()` to validate credentials\\n- Extracts username, roles, and JWT token from authentication result\\n- Sets ExecContext with user information and permissions\\n\\n**Authentication Handler Interface (arangod/Auth/Handler.h)**\\n- Abstract base class for pluggable authentication handlers\\n- Methods:\\n  - `authenticate(username, password)` - Authenticates and returns user roles\\n  - `readPermissions(username)` - Reads user permissions\\n  - Used by TokenCache for user validation\\n\\n### Summary of Key Components\\n\\n| Component | File | Role |\\n|-----------|------|------|\\n| UserManager | arangod/Auth/UserManager.h | Abstract user/permission access interface |\\n| UserManagerImpl | arangod/Auth/UserManagerImpl.h | Concrete implementation with caching |\\n| ExecContext | arangod/Utils/ExecContext.h | Execution context with permission tracking |\\n| AuthenticationFeature | arangod/GeneralServer/AuthenticationFeature.h | Configuration and initialization |\\n| RestAuthHandler | arangod/RestHandler/RestAuthHandler.h | JWT token generation endpoint |\\n| RestUsersHandler | arangod/RestHandler/RestUsersHandler.h | User management endpoint |\\n| TokenCache | arangod/Auth/TokenCache.h | Token validation and caching |\\n| AuthenticationOptions | arangod/GeneralServer/AuthenticationOptions.h | Configuration defaults |\\n| CommTask | arangod/GeneralServer/CommTask.h | HTTP request authentication processor |\\n| User | arangod/Auth/User.h | User entity with password and permission storage |\\n| Handler | arangod/Auth/Handler.h | Pluggable authentication interface |\\n| Common | arangod/Auth/Common.h | Auth level enums and utilities |\\n\\n### Design Patterns\\n\\n1. **Singleton Pattern**: AuthenticationFeature and ExecContext use singleton/thread-local patterns\\n2. **Strategy Pattern**: Handler interface allows different authentication backends\\n3. **Caching Strategy**: TokenCache uses LRU cache for JWT tokens and basic auth credentials\\n4. **Scope Guard Pattern**: ExecContextScope and ExecContextSuperuserScope manage context lifecycle\\n5. **Feature Pattern**: AuthenticationFeature integrates into application feature system\\n\\nThe architecture ensures secure authentication and fine-grained authorization at multiple layers, from HTTP request entry points through permission resolution for database operations.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
